LAW DEPARTMENT
LIST OF NOTARIES BY GOVERNMENT OF TAMIL NADU AND IN PRACTICE
AT THE BEGINNING OF THE YEAR 2023.
[G.O. (Ms) No. 73, Law (Administration), 31st January 2023, ¬î 17, சுபகிருது, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2054.]
No. II(2)/LAW/62(e)/2023.
In exercise of the powers conferred by Section 6 of the Notaries Act, 1952 (Central Act III of 1952), Governor of Tamil 
Nadu hereby publishes the following list of Notaries appointed by the government of Tamil nadu and practice at the beginning 
of the Year 2023.
